### рЯО® Arts & Cultural Opportunities

**City of West Hollywood 2026 Arts Grant Program**  
оИГThe City offers various grants for artists, including:оИД
- оИГArts Project Grant: Up to $20,000 for nonprofit arts organizations.оИД
- оИГCommunity Arts Grant: Up to $6,000 for individuals or nonprofits promoting BIPOC, LGBTQ+, and/or female artists.оИД
- оИГFilmmakers Grant: Up to $10,000 to support the completion of films already in post-production.оИД
- оИГTGI+ Arts Grant: Up to $6,500 for artists and nonprofits working with transgender, gender diverse, and intersex communities.оИД
- оИГWeHo Artist Grant: $6,000 annual grant for five local artists.оИД  
оИГApplication Deadline: July 1, 2025оИД  
рЯФЧ [Grant Details](https://wehoonline.com/west-hollywood-invites-applications-2026-arts-grants/)оИЖ

## рЯОѓ Strategy Tips (so you maximize ROI on attending)

1. **Show up early and hang until the end** вАФ most valuable connections happen during informal mingling.  
2. **Bring business cards / promo materials** (link to your tracks, reels) so people remember you.  
3. **Submit before deadlines** вАФ many showcases or opens have submission windows.  
4. **Be consistent** вАФ attend the same events weekly or monthly; familiarity helps.  
5. **Collaborate locally** вАФ with other songwriters, DJs, photographersвАФthose relationships tend to lead to work.
